31   /*
32    * Functionality to build the body of ASM MethodNode, except for `synchronized` and `try` expressions.
33    */
34   abstract class PlainBodyBuilder(cunit: CompilationUnit) extends PlainSkelBuilder(cunit) {
35 
36     import Primitives.TestOp
37 
38     /*  If the selector type has a member with the right name,
39      *  it is the host class; otherwise the symbol's owner.
40      */
41     def findHostClass(selector: Type, sym: Symbol) = selector member sym.name match {
42       case NoSymbol   => debuglog(s"Rejecting $selector as host class for $sym") ; sym.owner
43       case _          => selector.typeSymbol
44     }
45 
46     /* ---------------- helper utils for generating methods and code ---------------- */
47 
48     def emit(opc: Int): Unit = { mnode.visitInsn(opc) }
49 
50     def emitZeroOf(tk: BType): Unit = {
51       tk match {
52         case BOOL => bc.boolconst(false)
53         case BYTE  |
54              SHORT |
55              CHAR  |
56              INT     => bc.iconst(0)
57         case LONG    => bc.lconst(0)
58         case FLOAT   => bc.fconst(0)
59         case DOUBLE  => bc.dconst(0)
60         case UNIT    => ()
61         case _ => emit(asm.Opcodes.ACONST_NULL)
62       }
63     }
64 
65     /*
66      * Emits code that adds nothing to the operand stack.
67      * Two main cases: `tree` is an assignment,
68      * otherwise an `adapt()` to UNIT is performed if needed.
69      */
70     def genStat(tree: Tree): Unit = {
71       lineNumber(tree)
72 
73       tree match {
74         case Assign(lhs @ Select(_, _), rhs) =>
75           val isStatic = lhs.symbol.isStaticMember
76           if (!isStatic) { genLoadQualifier(lhs) }
77           genLoad(rhs, symInfoTK(lhs.symbol))
78           lineNumber(tree)
79           fieldStore(lhs.symbol)
80 
81         case Assign(lhs, rhs) =>
82           val s = lhs.symbol
83           val Local(tk, _, idx, _) = locals.getOrMakeLocal(s)
84           genLoad(rhs, tk)
85           lineNumber(tree)
86           bc.store(idx, tk)
87 
88         case _ =>
89           genLoad(tree, UNIT)
90       }
91     }
92 
93     def genThrow(expr: Tree): BType = {
94       val thrownKind = tpeTK(expr)
95       // `throw null` is valid although scala.Null (as defined in src/libray-aux) isn't a subtype of Throwable.
96       // Similarly for scala.Nothing (again, as defined in src/libray-aux).
97       assert(thrownKind.isNullType || thrownKind.isNothingType || thrownKind.asClassBType.isSubtypeOf(ThrowableReference))
98       genLoad(expr, thrownKind)
99       lineNumber(expr)
100       emit(asm.Opcodes.ATHROW) // ICode enters here into enterIgnoreMode, we'll rely instead on DCE at ClassNode level.
101 
102       RT_NOTHING // always returns the same, the invoker should know :)
103     }
104 
105     /* Generate code for primitive arithmetic operations. */
106     def genArithmeticOp(tree: Tree, code: Int): BType = tree match{
107       case Apply(fun @ Select(larg, _), args) =>
108       var resKind = tpeTK(larg)
109 
110       assert(resKind.isNumericType || (resKind == BOOL),
111              s"$resKind is not a numeric or boolean type [operation: ${fun.symbol}]")
112 
113       import ScalaPrimitivesOps._
114 
115       args match {
116         // unary operation
117         case Nil =>
118           genLoad(larg, resKind)
119           code match {
120             case POS => () // nothing
121             case NEG => bc.neg(resKind)
122             case NOT => bc.genPrimitiveArithmetic(Primitives.NOT, resKind)
123             case _ => abort(s"Unknown unary operation: ${fun.symbol.fullName} code: $code")
124           }
125 
126         // binary operation
127         case rarg :: Nil =>
128           resKind = tpeTK(larg).maxType(tpeTK(rarg))
129           if (isShiftOp(code) || isBitwiseOp(code)) {
130             assert(resKind.isIntegralType || (resKind == BOOL),
131                    s"$resKind incompatible with arithmetic modulo operation.")
132           }
133 
134           genLoad(larg, resKind)
135           genLoad(rarg, // check .NET size of shift arguments!
136                   if (isShiftOp(code)) INT else resKind)
137 
138           (code: @switch) match {
139             case ADD => bc add resKind
140             case SUB => bc sub resKind
141             case MUL => bc mul resKind
142             case DIV => bc div resKind
143             case MOD => bc rem resKind
144 
145             case OR  | XOR | AND => bc.genPrimitiveLogical(code, resKind)
146 
147             case LSL | LSR | ASR => bc.genPrimitiveShift(code, resKind)
148 
149             case _                   => abort(s"Unknown primitive: ${fun.symbol}[$code]")
150           }
151 
152         case _ =>
153           abort(s"Too many arguments for primitive function: $tree")
154       }
155       lineNumber(tree)
156       resKind
157     }
158 
159     /* Generate primitive array operations. */
160     def genArrayOp(tree: Tree, code: Int, expectedType: BType): BType = tree match{
161 
162       case Apply(Select(arrayObj, _), args) =>
163       import ScalaPrimitivesOps._
164       val k = tpeTK(arrayObj)
165       genLoad(arrayObj, k)
166       val elementType = typeOfArrayOp.getOrElse[bTypes.BType](code, abort(s"Unknown operation on arrays: $tree code: $code"))
167 
168       var generatedType = expectedType
169 
170       if (isArrayGet(code)) {
171         // load argument on stack
172         assert(args.length == 1, s"Too many arguments for array get operation: $tree");
173         genLoad(args.head, INT)
174         generatedType = k.asArrayBType.componentType
175         bc.aload(elementType)
176       }
177       else if (isArraySet(code)) {
178         args match {
179           case a1 :: a2 :: Nil =>
180             genLoad(a1, INT)
181             genLoad(a2)
182             // the following line should really be here, but because of bugs in erasure
183             // we pretend we generate whatever type is expected from us.
184             //generatedType = UNIT
185             bc.astore(elementType)
186           case _ =>
187             abort(s"Too many arguments for array set operation: $tree")
188         }
189       }
190       else {
191         generatedType = INT
192         emit(asm.Opcodes.ARRAYLENGTH)
193       }
194       lineNumber(tree)
195 
196       generatedType
197     }
198 
199     def genLoadIf(tree: If, expectedType: BType): BType = tree match{
200       case If(condp, thenp, elsep) =>
201 
202       val success = new asm.Label
203       val failure = new asm.Label
204 
205       val hasElse = !elsep.isEmpty
206       val postIf  = if (hasElse) new asm.Label else failure
207 
208       genCond(condp, success, failure, targetIfNoJump = success)
209       markProgramPoint(success)
210 
211       val thenKind      = tpeTK(thenp)
212       val elseKind      = if (!hasElse) UNIT else tpeTK(elsep)
213       def hasUnitBranch = (thenKind == UNIT || elseKind == UNIT) && expectedType == UNIT
214       val resKind       = if (hasUnitBranch) UNIT else tpeTK(tree)
215 
216       genLoad(thenp, resKind)
217       if (hasElse) { bc goTo postIf }
218       markProgramPoint(failure)
219       if (hasElse) {
220         genLoad(elsep, resKind)
221         markProgramPoint(postIf)
222       }
223 
224       resKind
225     }
226 
227     def genPrimitiveOp(tree: Apply, expectedType: BType): BType = tree match {
228       case Apply(fun @ Select(receiver, _), _) =>
229       val sym = tree.symbol
230 
231       val code = primitives.getPrimitive(tree, receiver.tpe)
232 
233       import ScalaPrimitivesOps._
234 
235       if (isArithmeticOp(code))                genArithmeticOp(tree, code)
236       else if (code == CONCAT) genStringConcat(tree)
237       else if (code == HASH)   genScalaHash(receiver)
238       else if (isArrayOp(code))                genArrayOp(tree, code, expectedType)
239       else if (isLogicalOp(code) || isComparisonOp(code)) {
240         val success, failure, after = new asm.Label
241         genCond(tree, success, failure, targetIfNoJump = success)
242         // success block
243         markProgramPoint(success)
244         bc boolconst true
245         bc goTo after
246         // failure block
247         markProgramPoint(failure)
248         bc boolconst false
249         // after
250         markProgramPoint(after)
251 
252         BOOL
253       }
254       else if (code == SYNCHRONIZED)
255         genSynchronized(tree, expectedType)
256       else if (isCoercion(code)) {
257         genLoad(receiver)
258         lineNumber(tree)
259         genCoercion(code)
260         coercionTo(code)
261       }
262       else abort(
263         s"Primitive operation not handled yet: ${sym.fullName}(${fun.symbol.simpleName}) at: ${tree.pos}"
264       )
265     }
266 
267     def genLoad(tree: Tree): Unit = {
268       genLoad(tree, tpeTK(tree))
269     }
270 
271     /* Generate code for trees that produce values on the stack */
272     def genLoad(tree: Tree, expectedType: BType): Unit = {
273       var generatedType = expectedType
274 
275       lineNumber(tree)
276 
277       tree match {
278         case lblDf @ LabelDef(_, _, _) => genLabelDef(lblDf, expectedType)
279 
280         case ValDef(_, `nme_THIS`, _, _) =>
281           debuglog("skipping trivial assign to _$this: " + tree)
282 
283         case ValDef(_, _, _, rhs) =>
284           val sym = tree.symbol
285           /* most of the time, !locals.contains(sym), unless the current activation of genLoad() is being called
286              while duplicating a finalizer that contains this ValDef. */
287           val loc = locals.getOrMakeLocal(sym)
288           val Local(tk, _, idx, isSynth) = loc
289           if (rhs == EmptyTree) { emitZeroOf(tk) }
290           else { genLoad(rhs, tk) }
291           val localVarStart = currProgramPoint()
292           bc.store(idx, tk)
293           if (!isSynth) { // there are case <synthetic> ValDef's emitted by patmat
294             varsInScope ::= (sym -> localVarStart)
295           }
296           generatedType = UNIT
297 
298         case t @ If(_, _, _) =>
299           generatedType = genLoadIf(t, expectedType)
300 
301         case r @ Return(_) =>
302           genReturn(r)
303           generatedType = expectedType
304 
305         case t @ Try(_, _, _) =>
306           generatedType = genLoadTry(t)
307 
308         case Throw(expr) =>
309           generatedType = genThrow(expr)
310 
311         case New(tpt) =>
312           abort(s"Unexpected New(${tpt.summaryString}/$tpt) reached GenBCode.\n" +
313                 "  Call was genLoad" + ((tree, expectedType)))
314 
315         case app @ Closure(env, call, functionalInterface) =>
316           val (fun, args) = call match {
317             case Apply(fun, args) => (fun, args)
318             case t @ Select(_, _) => (t, Nil)
319             case t @ Ident(_) => (t, Nil)
320           }
321 
322           if (!fun.symbol.isStaticMember) {
323             // load receiver of non-static implementation of lambda
324 
325             // darkdimius: I haven't found in spec `this` refference should go
326             // but I was able to derrive it by reading
327             // AbstractValidatingLambdaMetafactory.validateMetafactoryArgs
328 
329             val Select(prefix, _) = fun
330             genLoad(prefix)
331           }
332 
333           genLoadArguments(env, fun.symbol.info.paramTypes map toTypeKind)
334           generatedType = genInvokeDynamicLambda(NoSymbol, fun.symbol, env.size, functionalInterface)
335 
336         case app @ Apply(_, _) =>
337           generatedType = genApply(app, expectedType)
338 
339         case ApplyDynamic(qual, args) => sys.error("No invokedynamic support yet.")
340 
341         case This(qual) =>
342           val symIsModuleClass = tree.symbol.isModuleClass
343           assert(tree.symbol == claszSymbol || symIsModuleClass,
344                  s"Trying to access the this of another class: tree.symbol = ${tree.symbol}, class symbol = $claszSymbol compilation unit: $cunit")
345           if (symIsModuleClass && tree.symbol != claszSymbol) {
346             generatedType = genLoadModule(tree)
347           }
348           else {
349             mnode.visitVarInsn(asm.Opcodes.ALOAD, 0)
350             generatedType =
351               if (tree.symbol == ArrayClass) ObjectReference
352               else classBTypeFromSymbol(claszSymbol)
353           }
354 
355         case Select(Ident(`nme_EMPTY_PACKAGE_NAME`), module) =>
356           assert(tree.symbol.isModule, s"Selection of non-module from empty package: $tree sym: ${tree.symbol} at: ${tree.pos}")
357           genLoadModule(tree)
358 
359         case Select(qualifier, selector) =>
360           val sym = tree.symbol
361           generatedType = symInfoTK(sym)
362           val hostClass = findHostClass(qualifier.tpe, sym)
363           debuglog(s"Host class of $sym with qual $qualifier (${qualifier.tpe}) is $hostClass")
364           val qualSafeToElide = isQualifierSafeToElide(qualifier)
365 
366           def genLoadQualUnlessElidable(): Unit = { if (!qualSafeToElide) { genLoadQualifier(tree) } }
367 
368           if (sym.isModule) {
369             genLoadQualUnlessElidable()
370             genLoadModule(tree)
371           }
372           else if (sym.isStaticMember) {
373             genLoadQualUnlessElidable()
374             fieldLoad(sym, hostClass)
375           }
376           else {
377             genLoadQualifier(tree)
378             fieldLoad(sym, hostClass)
379           }
380 
381         case t @ Ident(name) =>
382           val sym = tree.symbol
383           val tk = symInfoTK(sym)
384           generatedType = tk
385 
386           val desugared = desugarIdent(t)
387           desugared match {
388             case None =>
389               if (!sym.hasPackageFlag) {
390                 if (sym.isModule) genLoadModule(sym)
391                 else locals.load(sym)
392               }
393             case Some(t) =>
394               genLoad(t, generatedType)
395           }
396 
397         case Literal(value) =>
398           if (value.tag != UnitTag) (value.tag, expectedType) match {
399             case (IntTag,   LONG  ) => bc.lconst(value.longValue);       generatedType = LONG
400             case (FloatTag, DOUBLE) => bc.dconst(value.doubleValue);     generatedType = DOUBLE
401             case (NullTag,  _     ) => bc.emit(asm.Opcodes.ACONST_NULL); generatedType = RT_NULL
402             case _                  => genConstant(value);               generatedType = tpeTK(tree)
403           }
404 
405         case blck @ Block(stats, expr) =>
406           if(stats.isEmpty)
407             genLoad(expr, expectedType)
408           else genBlock(blck, expectedType)
409 
410         case Typed(Super(_, _), _) => genLoad(This(claszSymbol), expectedType)
411 
412         case Typed(expr, _) => genLoad(expr, expectedType)
413 
414         case Assign(_, _) =>
415           generatedType = UNIT
416           genStat(tree)
417 
418         case av @ ArrayValue(_, _) =>
419           generatedType = genArrayValue(av)
420 
421         case mtch @ Match(_, _) =>
422           generatedType = genMatch(mtch)
423 
424         case EmptyTree => if (expectedType != UNIT) { emitZeroOf(expectedType) }
425 
426 
427         case t: TypeApply => // dotty specific
428           generatedType = genTypeApply(t)
429 
430         case _ => abort(s"Unexpected tree in genLoad: $tree/${tree.getClass} at: ${tree.pos}")
431       }
432 
433       // emit conversion
434       if (generatedType != expectedType) {
435         adapt(generatedType, expectedType)
436       }
437 
438     } // end of GenBCode.genLoad()
439 
440     // ---------------- field load and store ----------------
441 
442     /*
443      * must-single-thread
444      */
445     def fieldLoad( field: Symbol, hostClass: Symbol = null): Unit = {
446       fieldOp(field, isLoad = true,  hostClass)
447     }
448     /*
449      * must-single-thread
450      */
451     def fieldStore(field: Symbol, hostClass: Symbol = null): Unit = {
452       fieldOp(field, isLoad = false, hostClass)
453     }
454 
455     /*
456      * must-single-thread
457      */
458     private def fieldOp(field: Symbol, isLoad: Boolean, hostClass: Symbol): Unit = {
459       // LOAD_FIELD.hostClass , CALL_METHOD.hostClass , and #4283
460       val owner      =
461         if (hostClass == null) internalName(field.owner)
462         else                  internalName(hostClass)
463       val fieldJName = field.javaSimpleName.toString
464       val fieldDescr = symInfoTK(field).descriptor
465       val isStatic   = field.isStaticMember
466       val opc =
467         if (isLoad) { if (isStatic) asm.Opcodes.GETSTATIC else asm.Opcodes.GETFIELD }
468         else        { if (isStatic) asm.Opcodes.PUTSTATIC else asm.Opcodes.PUTFIELD }
469       mnode.visitFieldInsn(opc, owner, fieldJName, fieldDescr)
470 
471     }
472 
473     // ---------------- emitting constant values ----------------
474 
475     /*
476      * For const.tag in {ClazzTag, EnumTag}
477      *   must-single-thread
478      * Otherwise it's safe to call from multiple threads.
479      */
480     def genConstant(const: Constant): Unit = {
481       (const.tag/*: @switch*/) match {
482 
483         case BooleanTag => bc.boolconst(const.booleanValue)
484 
485         case ByteTag    => bc.iconst(const.byteValue)
486         case ShortTag   => bc.iconst(const.shortValue)
487         case CharTag    => bc.iconst(const.charValue)
488         case IntTag     => bc.iconst(const.intValue)
489 
490         case LongTag    => bc.lconst(const.longValue)
491         case FloatTag   => bc.fconst(const.floatValue)
492         case DoubleTag  => bc.dconst(const.doubleValue)
493 
494         case UnitTag    => ()
495 
496         case StringTag  =>
497           assert(const.value != null, const) // TODO this invariant isn't documented in `case class Constant`
498           mnode.visitLdcInsn(const.stringValue) // `stringValue` special-cases null, but not for a const with StringTag
499 
500         case NullTag    => emit(asm.Opcodes.ACONST_NULL)
501 
502         case ClazzTag   =>
503           val toPush: BType = {
504             toTypeKind(const.typeValue) match {
505               case kind: PrimitiveBType => boxedClassOfPrimitive(kind)
506               case kind => kind
507             }
508           }
509           mnode.visitLdcInsn(toPush.toASMType)
510 
511         case EnumTag   =>
512           val sym       = const.symbolValue
513           val ownerName = internalName(sym.owner)
514           val fieldName = sym.javaSimpleName.toString
515           val fieldDesc = toTypeKind(sym.tpe.underlying).descriptor
516           mnode.visitFieldInsn(
517             asm.Opcodes.GETSTATIC,
518             ownerName,
519             fieldName,
520             fieldDesc
521           )
522 
523         case _ => abort(s"Unknown constant value: $const")
524       }
525     }
526 
527     private def genLabelDef(lblDf: LabelDef, expectedType: BType, jumpTo: asm.Label = null): Unit = lblDf match {
528       case LabelDef(_, _, rhs) =>
529       // duplication of LabelDefs contained in `finally`-clauses is handled when emitting RETURN. No bookkeeping for that required here.
530       // no need to call index() over lblDf.params, on first access that magic happens (moreover, no LocalVariableTable entries needed for them).
531       markProgramPoint(programPoint(lblDf.symbol))
532       lineNumber(lblDf)
533       genLoad(rhs, expectedType)
534       if(jumpTo ne null) { // dotty
535         bc goTo jumpTo
536       }
537       else assert(!int.shouldEmitJumpAfterLabels) // scalac
538     }
539 
540     private def genReturn(r: Return) = r match{
541       case Return(expr) =>
542       val returnedKind = tpeTK(expr)
543       genLoad(expr, returnedKind)
544       adapt(returnedKind, returnType)
545       val saveReturnValue = (returnType != UNIT)
546       lineNumber(r)
547 
548       cleanups match {
549         case Nil =>
550           // not an assertion: !shouldEmitCleanup (at least not yet, pendingCleanups() may still have to run, and reset `shouldEmitCleanup`.
551           bc emitRETURN returnType
552         case nextCleanup :: rest =>
553           if (saveReturnValue) {
554             if (insideCleanupBlock) {
555               int.warning(r.pos, "Return statement found in finally-clause, discarding its return-value in favor of that of a more deeply nested return.")
556               bc drop returnType
557             } else {
558               // regarding return value, the protocol is: in place of a `return-stmt`, a sequence of `adapt, store, jump` are inserted.
559               if (earlyReturnVar == null) {
560                 earlyReturnVar = locals.makeLocal(returnType, "earlyReturnVar", expr.tpe, expr.pos)
561               }
562               locals.store(earlyReturnVar)
563             }
564           }
565           bc goTo nextCleanup
566           shouldEmitCleanup = true
567       }
568 
569     } // end of genReturn()
570 
571     def genTypeApply(t: TypeApply): BType = t match {
572       case TypeApply(fun@Select(obj, _), targs) =>
573 
574         val sym = fun.symbol
575         val cast = sym match {
576           case Object_isInstanceOf => false
577           case Object_asInstanceOf => true
578           case _ => abort(s"Unexpected type application $fun[sym: ${sym.fullName}] in: $t")
579         }
580 
581         val l = tpeTK(obj)
582         val r = tpeTK(targs.head)
583         genLoadQualifier(fun)
584 
585         // TODO @lry make pattern match
586         if (l.isPrimitive && r.isPrimitive)
587           genConversion(l, r, cast)
588         else if (l.isPrimitive) {
589           bc drop l
590           if (cast) {
591             mnode.visitTypeInsn(asm.Opcodes.NEW, classCastExceptionReference.internalName)
592             bc dup ObjectReference
593             emit(asm.Opcodes.ATHROW)
594           } else {
595             bc boolconst false
596           }
597         }
598         else if (r.isPrimitive && cast) {
599           abort(s"Erasure should have added an unboxing operation to prevent this cast. Tree: $t")
600         }
601         else if (r.isPrimitive) {
602           bc isInstance boxedClassOfPrimitive(r.asPrimitiveBType)
603         }
604         else {
605           assert(r.isRef, r) // ensure that it's not a method
606           genCast(r.asRefBType, cast)
607         }
608 
609         if (cast) r else BOOL
610     } // end of genTypeApply()
611 
612 
613     private def mkArrayConstructorCall(arr: ArrayBType, app: Apply, args: List[Tree]) = {
614       val dims     = arr.dimension
615       var elemKind = arr.elementType
616       val argsSize = args.length
617       if (argsSize > dims) {
618         error(app.pos, s"too many arguments for array constructor: found ${args.length} but array has only $dims dimension(s)")
619       }
620       if (argsSize < dims) {
621         /* In one step:
622          *   elemKind = new BType(BType.ARRAY, arr.off + argsSize, arr.len - argsSize)
623          * however the above does not enter a TypeName for each nested arrays in chrs.
624          */
625         for (i <- args.length until dims) elemKind = ArrayBType(elemKind)
626       }
627       genLoadArguments(args, List.fill(args.size)(INT))
628       (argsSize /*: @switch*/) match {
629         case 1 => bc newarray elemKind
630         case _ =>
631           val descr = ("[" * argsSize) + elemKind.descriptor // denotes the same as: arrayN(elemKind, argsSize).descriptor
632           mnode.visitMultiANewArrayInsn(descr, argsSize)
633       }
634     }
635 
636 
637     private def genApply(app: Apply, expectedType: BType): BType = {
638       var generatedType = expectedType
639       lineNumber(app)
640       app match {
641         case Apply(_, args) if isSyntheticArrayConstructor(app.symbol) =>
642           val List(elemClaz, Literal(c: Constant), ArrayValue(_, dims)) = args
643 
644           generatedType = toTypeKind(c.typeValue)
645           mkArrayConstructorCall(generatedType.asArrayBType, app, dims)
646         case Apply(t :TypeApply, _) =>
647 
648           generatedType = genTypeApply(t)
649 
650         // 'super' call: Note: since constructors are supposed to
651         // return an instance of what they construct, we have to take
652         // special care. On JVM they are 'void', and Scala forbids (syntactically)
653         // to call super constructors explicitly and/or use their 'returned' value.
654         // therefore, we can ignore this fact, and generate code that leaves nothing
655         // on the stack (contrary to what the type in the AST says).
656         case Apply(fun @ Select(Super(_, mix), _), args) =>
657           val invokeStyle = InvokeStyle.Super
658           // if (fun.symbol.isConstructor) Static(true) else SuperCall(mix);
659           mnode.visitVarInsn(asm.Opcodes.ALOAD, 0)
660           genLoadArguments(args, paramTKs(app))
661           genCallMethod(fun.symbol, invokeStyle, pos = app.pos)
662           generatedType = asmMethodType(fun.symbol).returnType
663 
664         // 'new' constructor call: Note: since constructors are
665         // thought to return an instance of what they construct,
666         // we have to 'simulate' it by DUPlicating the freshly created
667         // instance (on JVM, <init> methods return VOID).
668         case Apply(fun @ Select(New(tpt), `nme_CONSTRUCTOR`), args) =>
669           val ctor = fun.symbol
670           assert(ctor.isClassConstructor, s"'new' call to non-constructor: ${ctor.name}")
671 
672           generatedType = toTypeKind(tpt)
673           assert(generatedType.isRef, s"Non reference type cannot be instantiated: $generatedType")
674 
675           generatedType match {
676             case arr: ArrayBType =>
677               mkArrayConstructorCall(arr, app, args)
678 
679             case rt: ClassBType =>
680               assert(classBTypeFromSymbol(ctor.owner) == rt, s"Symbol ${ctor.owner.fullName} is different from $rt")
681               mnode.visitTypeInsn(asm.Opcodes.NEW, rt.internalName)
682               bc dup generatedType
683               genLoadArguments(args, paramTKs(app))
684               genCallMethod(ctor, InvokeStyle.Special)
685 
686             case _ =>
687               abort(s"Cannot instantiate $tpt of kind: $generatedType")
688           }
689 
690         case Apply(fun, List(expr)) if isBox(fun.symbol) =>
691           val nativeKind = tpeTK(expr)
692           genLoad(expr, nativeKind)
693           val MethodNameAndType(mname, methodType) = asmBoxTo(nativeKind)
694           bc.invokestatic(BoxesRunTime.internalName, mname, methodType.descriptor)
695           generatedType = boxResultType(fun.symbol) // was toTypeKind(fun.symbol.tpe.resultType)
696 
697         case Apply(fun, List(expr)) if isUnbox(fun.symbol) =>
698           genLoad(expr)
699           val boxType = unboxResultType(fun.symbol) // was toTypeKind(fun.symbol.owner.linkedClassOfClass.tpe)
700           generatedType = boxType
701           val MethodNameAndType(mname, methodType) = asmUnboxTo(boxType)
702           bc.invokestatic(BoxesRunTime.internalName, mname, methodType.descriptor)
703 
704         case app @ Apply(fun, args) =>
705           val sym = fun.symbol
706 
707           if (sym.isLabel) {  // jump to a label
708             genLoadLabelArguments(args, labelDef(sym), app.pos)
709             bc goTo programPoint(sym)
710           } else if (isPrimitive(fun)) { // primitive method call
711             generatedType = genPrimitiveOp(app, expectedType)
712           } else {  // normal method call
713 
714             def genNormalMethodCall(): Unit = {
715 
716               val invokeStyle =
717                 if (sym.isStaticMember) InvokeStyle.Static
718                 else if (sym.isPrivate || sym.isClassConstructor) InvokeStyle.Special
719                 else InvokeStyle.Virtual
720 
721               if (invokeStyle.hasInstance) {
722                 genLoadQualifier(fun)
723               }
724 
725               genLoadArguments(args, paramTKs(app))
726 
727               // In "a couple cases", squirrel away a extra information (hostClass, targetTypeKind). TODO Document what "in a couple cases" refers to.
728               var hostClass:      Symbol = null
729 
730               fun match {
731                 case Select(qual, _) if isArrayClone(fun) && invokeStyle.isVirtual =>
732                   val targetTypeKind = tpeTK(qual)
733                   val target: String = targetTypeKind.asRefBType.classOrArrayType
734                   bc.invokevirtual(target, "clone", "()Ljava/lang/Object;")
735                   generatedType = targetTypeKind
736 
737                 case Select(qual, _) =>
738                   val qualSym = findHostClass(qual.tpe, sym)
739 
740                   hostClass = qualSym
741                   if (qual.tpe.typeSymbol != qualSym) {
742                       log(s"Precisified host class for $sym from ${qual.tpe.typeSymbol.fullName} to ${qualSym.fullName}")
743                     }
744                   genCallMethod(sym, invokeStyle, hostClass, app.pos)
745                   generatedType = asmMethodType(sym).returnType
746 
747                 case _ =>
748                   genCallMethod(sym, invokeStyle, hostClass, app.pos)
749                   generatedType = asmMethodType(sym).returnType
750 
751               }
752             } // end of genNormalMethodCall()
753 
754             genNormalMethodCall()
755 
756           }
757 
758       }
759 
760       generatedType
761     } // end of genApply()
762 
763     private def genArrayValue(av: ArrayValue): BType = av match {
764       case ArrayValue(tpt, elems) =>
765       val ArrayValue(tpt, elems) = av
766 
767       lineNumber(av)
768       genArray(elems, tpt)
769     }
770 
771     private def genArray(elems: List[Tree], elemType: Type): BType = {
772       val elmKind       = toTypeKind(elemType)
773       val generatedType = ArrayBType(elmKind)
774 
775       bc iconst   elems.length
776       bc newarray elmKind
777 
778       var i = 0
779       var rest = elems
780       while (!rest.isEmpty) {
781         bc dup     generatedType
782         bc iconst  i
783         genLoad(rest.head, elmKind)
784         bc astore  elmKind
785         rest = rest.tail
786         i = i + 1
787       }
788 
789       generatedType
790     }
791 
792     /*
793      * A Match node contains one or more case clauses,
794      * each case clause lists one or more Int values to use as keys, and a code block.
795      * Except the "default" case clause which (if it exists) doesn't list any Int key.
796      *
797      * On a first pass over the case clauses, we flatten the keys and their targets (the latter represented with asm.Labels).
798      * That representation allows JCodeMethodV to emit a lookupswitch or a tableswitch.
799      *
800      * On a second pass, we emit the switch blocks, one for each different target.
801      */
802     private def genMatch(tree: Match): BType = tree match {
803       case Match(selector, cases) =>
804       lineNumber(tree)
805       genLoad(selector, INT)
806       val generatedType = tpeTK(tree)
807 
808       var flatKeys: List[Int]       = Nil
809       var targets:  List[asm.Label] = Nil
810       var default:  asm.Label       = null
811       var switchBlocks: List[(asm.Label, Tree)] = Nil
812 
813       // collect switch blocks and their keys, but don't emit yet any switch-block.
814       for (caze @ CaseDef(pat, guard, body) <- cases) {
815         assert(guard == EmptyTree, guard)
816         val switchBlockPoint = new asm.Label
817         switchBlocks ::= (switchBlockPoint, body)
818         pat match {
819           case Literal(value) =>
820             flatKeys ::= value.intValue
821             targets  ::= switchBlockPoint
822           case Ident(`nme_WILDCARD`) =>
823             assert(default == null, s"multiple default targets in a Match node, at ${tree.pos}")
824             default = switchBlockPoint
825           case Alternative(alts) =>
826             alts foreach {
827               case Literal(value) =>
828                 flatKeys ::= value.intValue
829                 targets  ::= switchBlockPoint
830               case _ =>
831                 abort(s"Invalid alternative in alternative pattern in Match node: $tree at: ${tree.pos}")
832             }
833           case _ =>
834             abort(s"Invalid pattern in Match node: $tree at: ${tree.pos}")
835         }
836       }
837 
838       bc.emitSWITCH(mkArrayReverse(flatKeys), mkArrayL(targets.reverse), default, MIN_SWITCH_DENSITY)
839 
840       // emit switch-blocks.
841       val postMatch = new asm.Label
842       for (sb <- switchBlocks.reverse) {
843         val (caseLabel, caseBody) = sb
844         markProgramPoint(caseLabel)
845         genLoad(caseBody, generatedType)
846         bc goTo postMatch
847       }
848 
849       markProgramPoint(postMatch)
850       generatedType
851     }
852 
853     def genBlock(tree: Block, expectedType: BType) = tree match {
854       case Block(stats, expr) =>
855 
856 
857       def genNormalBlock =  {
858         val savedScope = varsInScope
859         varsInScope = Nil
860         stats foreach genStat
861         genLoad(expr, expectedType)
862         val end = currProgramPoint()
863         if (emitVars) {
864           // add entries to LocalVariableTable JVM attribute
865           for ((sym, start) <- varsInScope.reverse) {
866             emitLocalVarScope(sym, start, end)
867           }
868         }
869         varsInScope = savedScope
870       }
871 
872       if(!int.shouldEmitJumpAfterLabels) genNormalBlock
873       else {
874         val (prefixLabels: List[LabelDef] @unchecked, stats1) = stats.span {
875           case t@LabelDef(_, _, _) => true
876           case _ => false
877         }
878         assert(stats1.isEmpty || prefixLabels.isEmpty)
879         if (!prefixLabels.isEmpty) {
880           val startLocation = new asm.Label
881           val breakLocation = new asm.Label
882           bc goTo startLocation
883           prefixLabels.foreach{ lblDf => labelDef.+=(lblDf.symbol -> lblDf)}
884           prefixLabels.foreach{ lblDf => genLabelDef(lblDf, tpeTK(lblDf), breakLocation)}
885           markProgramPoint(startLocation)
886           val generated = tpeTK(expr)
887           genLoad(expr, generated)
888           markProgramPoint(breakLocation)
889           if (generated != expectedType)
890             adapt(generated, expectedType)
891         }
892         else genNormalBlock
893       }
894     }
895 
896     def adapt(from: BType, to: BType): Unit = {
897       if (!from.conformsTo(to)) {
898         to match {
899           case UNIT => bc drop from
900           case _    => bc.emitT2T(from, to)
901         }
902       } else if (from.isNothingType) {
903         /* There are two possibilities for from.isNothingType: emitting a "throw e" expressions and
904          * loading a (phantom) value of type Nothing.
905          *
906          * The Nothing type in Scala's type system does not exist in the JVM. In bytecode, Nothing
907          * is mapped to scala.runtime.Nothing$. To the JVM, a call to Predef.??? looks like it would
908          * return an object of type Nothing$. We need to do something with that phantom object on
909          * the stack. "Phantom" because it never exists: such methods always throw, but the JVM does
910          * not know that.
911          *
912          * Note: The two verifiers (old: type inference, new: type checking) have different
913          * requirements. Very briefly:
914          *
915          * Old (http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.10.2.1): at
916          * each program point, no matter what branches were taken to get there
917          *   - Stack is same size and has same typed values
918          *   - Local and stack values need to have consistent types
919          *   - In practice, the old verifier seems to ignore unreachable code and accept any
920          *     instructions after an ATHROW. For example, there can be another ATHROW (without
921          *     loading another throwable first).
922          *
923          * New (http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.10.1)
924          *   - Requires consistent stack map frames. GenBCode generates stack frames if -target:jvm-1.6
925          *     or higher.
926          *   - In practice: the ASM library computes stack map frames for us (ClassWriter). Emitting
927          *     correct frames after an ATHROW is probably complex, so ASM uses the following strategy:
928          *       - Every time when generating an ATHROW, a new basic block is started.
929          *       - During classfile writing, such basic blocks are found to be dead: no branches go there
930          *       - Eliminating dead code would probably require complex shifts in the output byte buffer
931          *       - But there's an easy solution: replace all code in the dead block with with
932          *         `nop; nop; ... nop; athrow`, making sure the bytecode size stays the same
933          *       - The corresponding stack frame can be easily generated: on entering a dead the block,
934          *         the frame requires a single Throwable on the stack.
935          *       - Since there are no branches to the dead block, the frame requirements are never violated.
936          *
937          * To summarize the above: it does matter what we emit after an ATHROW.
938          *
939          * NOW: if we end up here because we emitted a load of a (phantom) value of type Nothing$,
940          * there was no ATHROW emitted. So, we have to make the verifier happy and do something
941          * with that value. Since Nothing$ extends Throwable, the easiest is to just emit an ATHROW.
942          *
943          * If we ended up here because we generated a "throw e" expression, we know the last
944          * emitted instruction was an ATHROW. As explained above, it is OK to emit a second ATHROW,
945          * the verifiers will be happy.
946          */
947         if (lastInsn.getOpcode != asm.Opcodes.ATHROW)
948           emit(asm.Opcodes.ATHROW)
949       } else if (from.isNullType) {
950         /* After loading an expression of type `scala.runtime.Null$`, introduce POP; ACONST_NULL.
951          * This is required to pass the verifier: in Scala's type system, Null conforms to any
952          * reference type. In bytecode, the type Null is represented by scala.runtime.Null$, which
953          * is not a subtype of all reference types. Example:
954          *
955          *   def nl: Null = null // in bytecode, nl has return type scala.runtime.Null$
956          *   val a: String = nl  // OK for Scala but not for the JVM, scala.runtime.Null$ does not conform to String
957          *
958          * In order to fix the above problem, the value returned by nl is dropped and ACONST_NULL is
959          * inserted instead - after all, an expression of type scala.runtime.Null$ can only be null.
960          */
961         if (lastInsn.getOpcode != asm.Opcodes.ACONST_NULL) {
962           bc drop from
963           emit(asm.Opcodes.ACONST_NULL)
964         }
965       }
966       else (from, to) match  {
967         case (BYTE, LONG) | (SHORT, LONG) | (CHAR, LONG) | (INT, LONG) => bc.emitT2T(INT, LONG)
968         case _ => ()
969       }
970     }
971 
972     /* Emit code to Load the qualifier of `tree` on top of the stack. */
973     def genLoadQualifier(tree: Tree): Unit = {
974       lineNumber(tree)
975       tree match {
976         case Select(qualifier, _) => genLoad(qualifier)
977         case t: Ident             => // dotty specific
978           desugarIdent(t) match {
979             case Some(sel) => genLoadQualifier(sel)
980             case None =>
981               assert(t.symbol.owner == this.claszSymbol)
982           }
983         case _                    => abort(s"Unknown qualifier $tree")
984       }
985     }
986 
987     /* Generate code that loads args into label parameters. */
988     def genLoadLabelArguments(args: List[Tree], lblDef: LabelDef, gotoPos: Position) = lblDef match {
989       case LabelDef(_, param, _) =>
990 
991       val aps = {
992         val params: List[Symbol] = param
993         assert(args.length == params.length, s"Wrong number of arguments in call to label at: $gotoPos")
994 
995         def isTrivial(kv: (Tree, Symbol)) = kv match {
996           case (This(_), p) if p.name == nme_THIS     => true
997           case (arg @ Ident(_), p) if arg.symbol == p => true
998           case _                                      => false
999         }
1000 
1001         (args zip params) filterNot isTrivial
1002       }
1003 
1004       // first push *all* arguments. This makes sure muliple uses of the same labelDef-var will all denote the (previous) value.
1005       aps foreach { case (arg, param) => genLoad(arg, locals(param).tk) } // `locals` is known to contain `param` because `genDefDef()` visited `labelDefsAtOrUnder`
1006 
1007       // second assign one by one to the LabelDef's variables.
1008       aps.reverse foreach {
1009         case (_, param) =>
1010           // TODO FIXME a "this" param results from tail-call xform. If so, the `else` branch seems perfectly fine. And the `then` branch must be wrong.
1011           if (param.name == nme_THIS) mnode.visitVarInsn(asm.Opcodes.ASTORE, 0)
1012           else locals.store(param)
1013       }
1014 
1015     }
1016 
1017     def genLoadArguments(args: List[Tree], btpes: List[BType]): Unit = {
1018       (args zip btpes) foreach { case (arg, btpe) => genLoad(arg, btpe) }
1019     }
1020 
1021     def genLoadModule(tree: Tree): BType = {
1022       val module = (
1023         if (!tree.symbol.isPackageClass) tree.symbol
1024         else tree.symbol.info.member(nme_PACKAGE) match {
1025           case NoSymbol => abort(s"SI-5604: Cannot use package as value: $tree")
1026           case s        => abort(s"SI-5604: found package class where package object expected: $tree")
1027         }
1028       )
1029       lineNumber(tree)
1030       genLoadModule(module)
1031       symInfoTK(module)
1032     }
1033 
1034     def genLoadModule(module: Symbol): Unit = {
1035       def inStaticMethod = methSymbol != null && methSymbol.isStaticMember
1036       if (claszSymbol == module.moduleClass && jMethodName != "readResolve" && !inStaticMethod) {
1037         mnode.visitVarInsn(asm.Opcodes.ALOAD, 0)
1038       } else {
1039         val mbt = symInfoTK(module).asClassBType
1040         mnode.visitFieldInsn(
1041           asm.Opcodes.GETSTATIC,
1042           mbt.internalName /* + "$" */ ,
1043           MODULE_INSTANCE_FIELD,
1044           mbt.descriptor // for nostalgics: toTypeKind(module.tpe).descriptor
1045         )
1046       }
1047     }

1049     def genConversion(from: BType, to: BType, cast: Boolean): Unit = {
1050       if (cast) { bc.emitT2T(from, to) }
1051       else {
1052         bc drop from
1053         bc boolconst (from == to)
1054       }
1055     }
1056 
1057     def genCast(to: RefBType, cast: Boolean): Unit = {
1058       if (cast) { bc checkCast  to }
1059       else      { bc isInstance to }
1060     }

1062     /* Is the given symbol a primitive operation? */
1063     def isPrimitive(fun: Tree): Boolean = {
1064       primitives.isPrimitive(fun)
1065     }

1067     /* Generate coercion denoted by "code" */
1068     def genCoercion(code: Int): Unit = {
1069       import ScalaPrimitivesOps._
1070       (code: @switch) match {
1071         case B2B | S2S | C2C | I2I | L2L | F2F | D2D => ()
1072         case _ =>
1073           val from = coercionFrom(code)
1074           val to   = coercionTo(code)
1075           bc.emitT2T(from, to)
1076       }
1077     }

1079     def genStringConcat(tree: Tree): BType = {
1080       lineNumber(tree)
1081       liftStringConcat(tree) match {
1082 
1083         // Optimization for expressions of the form "" + x.  We can avoid the StringBuilder.
1084         case List(Literal(Constant("")), arg) =>
1085           genLoad(arg, ObjectReference)
1086           genCallMethod(String_valueOf, InvokeStyle.Static)
1087 
1088         case concatenations =>
1089           bc.genStartConcat
1090           for (elem <- concatenations) {
1091             val loadedElem = elem match {
1092               case Apply(boxOp, value :: Nil) if isBox(boxOp.symbol) =>
1093                 // Eliminate boxing of primitive values. Boxing is introduced by erasure because
1094                 // there's only a single synthetic `+` method "added" to the string class.
1095                 value
1096 
1097               case _ => elem
1098             }
1099             val elemType = tpeTK(loadedElem)
1100             genLoad(loadedElem, elemType)
1101             bc.genConcat(elemType)
1102           }
1103           bc.genEndConcat
1104 
1105       }
1106 
1107       StringRef
1108     }
1109 
1110     def genCallMethod(method: Symbol, style: InvokeStyle, hostClass0: Symbol = null, pos: Position = NoPosition): Unit = {
1111 
1112       val siteSymbol = claszSymbol
1113       val hostSymbol = if (hostClass0 == null) method.owner else hostClass0
1114       val methodOwner = method.owner
1115       // info calls so that types are up to date; erasure may add lateINTERFACE to traits
1116       hostSymbol.info ; methodOwner.info
1117 
1118       def needsInterfaceCall(sym: Symbol) = (
1119            sym.isInterface
1120         || sym.isJavaDefined && sym.isNonBottomSubClass(ClassfileAnnotationClass)
1121       )
1122 
1123       // whether to reference the type of the receiver or
1124       // the type of the method owner
1125       val useMethodOwner = (
1126            !style.isVirtual
1127         || hostSymbol.isBottomClass
1128         || methodOwner == ObjectClass
1129       )
1130       val receiver = if (useMethodOwner) methodOwner else hostSymbol
1131       val jowner   = internalName(receiver)
1132       val jname    = method.javaSimpleName.toString
1133       val bmType   = asmMethodType(method)
1134       val mdescr   = bmType.descriptor
1135 
1136       def initModule(): Unit = {
1137         // we initialize the MODULE$ field immediately after the super ctor
1138         if (!isModuleInitialized &&
1139             jMethodName == INSTANCE_CONSTRUCTOR_NAME &&
1140             jname == INSTANCE_CONSTRUCTOR_NAME &&
1141           siteSymbol.isStaticModuleClass) {
1142           isModuleInitialized = true
1143           mnode.visitVarInsn(asm.Opcodes.ALOAD, 0)
1144           mnode.visitFieldInsn(
1145             asm.Opcodes.PUTSTATIC,
1146             thisName,
1147             MODULE_INSTANCE_FIELD,
1148             "L" + thisName + ";"
1149           )
1150         }
1151       }
1152 
1153       if (style.isStatic)                 { bc.invokestatic   (jowner, jname, mdescr) }
1154       else if (style.isSpecial)           { bc.invokespecial  (jowner, jname, mdescr) }
1155       else if (style.isVirtual) {
1156         if (needsInterfaceCall(receiver)) { bc.invokeinterface(jowner, jname, mdescr) }
1157         else                              { bc.invokevirtual  (jowner, jname, mdescr) }
1158       }
1159       else {
1160         assert(style.isSuper, s"An unknown InvokeStyle: $style")
1161         bc.invokespecial(jowner, jname, mdescr)
1162         initModule()
1163       }
1164 
1165     } // end of genCallMethod()
1166 
1167     /* Generate the scala ## method. */
1168     def genScalaHash(tree: Tree): BType = {
1169       genLoadModule(ScalaRunTimeModule) // TODO why load ScalaRunTimeModule if ## has InvokeStyle of Static(false) ?
1170       genLoad(tree, ObjectReference)
1171       genCallMethod(hashMethodSym, InvokeStyle.Static)
1172 
1173       INT
1174     }
1175 
1176     /*
1177      * Returns a list of trees that each should be concatenated, from left to right.
1178      * It turns a chained call like "a".+("b").+("c") into a list of arguments.
1179      */
1180     def liftStringConcat(tree: Tree): List[Tree] = tree match {
1181       case tree @ Apply(fun @ Select(larg, method), rarg) =>
1182         if (isPrimitive(fun) &&
1183             primitives.getPrimitive(tree, larg.tpe) == ScalaPrimitivesOps.CONCAT)
1184           liftStringConcat(larg) ::: rarg
1185         else
1186           tree :: Nil
1187       case _ =>
1188         tree :: Nil
1189     }
1190 
1191     /* Emit code to compare the two top-most stack values using the 'op' operator. */
1192     private def genCJUMP(success: asm.Label, failure: asm.Label, op: TestOp, tk: BType, targetIfNoJump: asm.Label): Unit = {
1193       if (targetIfNoJump == success) genCJUMP(failure, success, op.negate(), tk, targetIfNoJump)
1194       else {
1195         if (tk.isIntSizedType) { // BOOL, BYTE, CHAR, SHORT, or INT
1196           bc.emitIF_ICMP(op, success)
1197         } else if (tk.isRef) { // REFERENCE(_) | ARRAY(_)
1198           bc.emitIF_ACMP(op, success)
1199         } else {
1200           import Primitives._
1201           (tk: @unchecked) match {
1202             case LONG   => emit(asm.Opcodes.LCMP)
1203             case FLOAT  =>
1204               if (op == LT || op == LE) emit(asm.Opcodes.FCMPG)
1205               else emit(asm.Opcodes.FCMPL)
1206             case DOUBLE =>
1207               if (op == LT || op == LE) emit(asm.Opcodes.DCMPG)
1208               else emit(asm.Opcodes.DCMPL)
1209           }
1210           bc.emitIF(op, success)
1211         }
1212         if (targetIfNoJump != failure) bc goTo failure
1213       }
1214     }
1215 
1216     /* Emits code to compare (and consume) stack-top and zero using the 'op' operator */
1217     private def genCZJUMP(success: asm.Label, failure: asm.Label, op: TestOp, tk: BType, targetIfNoJump: asm.Label): Unit = {
1218       import Primitives._
1219       if (targetIfNoJump == success) genCZJUMP(failure, success, op.negate(), tk, targetIfNoJump)
1220       else {
1221         if (tk.isIntSizedType) { // BOOL, BYTE, CHAR, SHORT, or INT
1222           bc.emitIF(op, success)
1223         } else if (tk.isRef) { // REFERENCE(_) | ARRAY(_)
1224           (op: @unchecked) match { // references are only compared with EQ and NE
1225             case EQ => bc emitIFNULL    success
1226             case NE => bc emitIFNONNULL success
1227           }
1228         } else {
1229           (tk: @unchecked) match {
1230             case LONG   =>
1231               emit(asm.Opcodes.LCONST_0)
1232               emit(asm.Opcodes.LCMP)
1233             case FLOAT  =>
1234               emit(asm.Opcodes.FCONST_0)
1235               if (op == LT || op == LE) emit(asm.Opcodes.FCMPG)
1236               else emit(asm.Opcodes.FCMPL)
1237             case DOUBLE =>
1238               emit(asm.Opcodes.DCONST_0)
1239               if (op == LT || op == LE) emit(asm.Opcodes.DCMPG)
1240               else emit(asm.Opcodes.DCMPL)
1241           }
1242           bc.emitIF(op, success)
1243         }
1244         if (targetIfNoJump != failure) bc goTo failure
1245       }
1246     }
1247 
1248     def testOpForPrimitive(primitiveCode: Int) = (primitiveCode: @switch) match {
1249        case ScalaPrimitivesOps.ID => Primitives.EQ
1250        case ScalaPrimitivesOps.NI => Primitives.NE
1251        case ScalaPrimitivesOps.EQ => Primitives.EQ
1252        case ScalaPrimitivesOps.NE => Primitives.NE
1253        case ScalaPrimitivesOps.LT => Primitives.LT
1254        case ScalaPrimitivesOps.LE => Primitives.LE
1255        case ScalaPrimitivesOps.GE => Primitives.GE
1256        case ScalaPrimitivesOps.GT => Primitives.GT
1257      }
1258 
1259     /*
1260      * Generate code for conditional expressions.
1261      * The jump targets success/failure of the test are `then-target` and `else-target` resp.
1262      */
1263     private def genCond(tree: Tree, success: asm.Label, failure: asm.Label, targetIfNoJump: asm.Label): Unit = {
1264 
1265       def genComparisonOp(l: Tree, r: Tree, code: Int): Unit = {
1266         val op = testOpForPrimitive(code)
1267         val nonNullSide = if (ScalaPrimitivesOps.isReferenceEqualityOp(code)) ifOneIsNull(l, r) else null
1268         if (nonNullSide != null) {
1269           // special-case reference (in)equality test for null (null eq x, x eq null)
1270           genLoad(nonNullSide, ObjectReference)
1271           genCZJUMP(success, failure, op, ObjectReference, targetIfNoJump)
1272         } else {
1273           val tk = tpeTK(l).maxType(tpeTK(r))
1274           genLoad(l, tk)
1275           genLoad(r, tk)
1276           genCJUMP(success, failure, op, tk, targetIfNoJump)
1277         }
1278       }
1279 
1280       def loadAndTestBoolean() = {
1281         genLoad(tree, BOOL)
1282         genCZJUMP(success, failure, Primitives.NE, BOOL, targetIfNoJump)
1283       }
1284 
1285       lineNumber(tree)
1286       tree match {
1287 
1288         case tree @ Apply(fun, args) if isPrimitive(fun) =>
1289           import ScalaPrimitivesOps.{ ZNOT, ZAND, ZOR, EQ }
1290 
1291           // lhs and rhs of test
1292           lazy val Select(lhs, _) = fun
1293           val rhs = if (args.isEmpty) EmptyTree else args.head // args.isEmpty only for ZNOT
1294 
1295           def genZandOrZor(and: Boolean): Unit = {
1296             // reaching "keepGoing" indicates the rhs should be evaluated too (ie not short-circuited).
1297             val keepGoing = new asm.Label
1298 
1299             if (and) genCond(lhs, keepGoing, failure, targetIfNoJump = keepGoing)
1300             else     genCond(lhs, success,   keepGoing, targetIfNoJump = keepGoing)
1301 
1302             markProgramPoint(keepGoing)
1303             genCond(rhs, success, failure, targetIfNoJump)
1304           }
1305 
1306           primitives.getPrimitive(tree, lhs.tpe) match {
1307             case ZNOT   => genCond(lhs, failure, success, targetIfNoJump)
1308             case ZAND   => genZandOrZor(and = true)
1309             case ZOR    => genZandOrZor(and = false)
1310             case code   =>
1311               if (ScalaPrimitivesOps.isUniversalEqualityOp(code) && tpeTK(lhs).isClass) {
1312                 // rewrite `==` to null tests and `equals`. not needed for arrays (`equals` is reference equality).
1313                 if (code == EQ) genEqEqPrimitive(lhs, rhs, success, failure, targetIfNoJump)
1314                 else            genEqEqPrimitive(lhs, rhs, failure, success, targetIfNoJump)
1315               } else if (ScalaPrimitivesOps.isComparisonOp(code)) {
1316                 genComparisonOp(lhs, rhs, code)
1317               } else
1318                 loadAndTestBoolean()
1319           }
1320 
1321         case _ => loadAndTestBoolean()
1322       }
1323 
1324     } // end of genCond()
1325 
1326     /*
1327      * Generate the "==" code for object references. It is equivalent of
1328      * if (l eq null) r eq null else l.equals(r);
1329      *
1330      * @param l       left-hand-side  of the '=='
1331      * @param r       right-hand-side of the '=='
1332      */
1333     def genEqEqPrimitive(l: Tree, r: Tree, success: asm.Label, failure: asm.Label, targetIfNoJump: asm.Label): Unit = {
1334 
1335       /* True if the equality comparison is between values that require the use of the rich equality
1336        * comparator (scala.runtime.Comparator.equals). This is the case when either side of the
1337        * comparison might have a run-time type subtype of java.lang.Number or java.lang.Character.
1338        * When it is statically known that both sides are equal and subtypes of Number of Character,
1339        * not using the rich equality is possible (their own equals method will do ok.)
1340        */
1341       val mustUseAnyComparator: Boolean = {
1342         val areSameFinals = l.tpe.isFinalType && r.tpe.isFinalType && (l.tpe =:= r.tpe)
1343 
1344         !areSameFinals && isMaybeBoxed(l.tpe.typeSymbol) && isMaybeBoxed(r.tpe.typeSymbol)
1345       }
1346 
1347       if (mustUseAnyComparator) {
1348         val equalsMethod: Symbol = {
1349           if (l.tpe <:< BoxedNumberClass.tpe) {
1350             if (r.tpe <:< BoxedNumberClass.tpe) externalEqualsNumNum
1351             else if (r.tpe <:< BoxedCharacterClass.tpe) externalEqualsNumChar
1352             else externalEqualsNumObject
1353           } else externalEquals
1354         }
1355 
1356         genLoad(l, ObjectReference)
1357         genLoad(r, ObjectReference)
1358         genCallMethod(equalsMethod, InvokeStyle.Static)
1359         genCZJUMP(success, failure, Primitives.NE, BOOL, targetIfNoJump)
1360       }
1361       else {
1362         if (isNull(l)) {
1363           // null == expr -> expr eq null
1364           genLoad(r, ObjectReference)
1365           genCZJUMP(success, failure, Primitives.EQ, ObjectReference, targetIfNoJump)
1366         } else if (isNull(r)) {
1367           // expr == null -> expr eq null
1368           genLoad(l, ObjectReference)
1369           genCZJUMP(success, failure, Primitives.EQ, ObjectReference, targetIfNoJump)
1370         } else if (isNonNullExpr(l)) {
1371           // SI-7852 Avoid null check if L is statically non-null.
1372           genLoad(l, ObjectReference)
1373           genLoad(r, ObjectReference)
1374           genCallMethod(Object_equals, InvokeStyle.Virtual)
1375           genCZJUMP(success, failure, Primitives.NE, BOOL, targetIfNoJump)
1376         } else {
1377           // l == r -> if (l eq null) r eq null else l.equals(r)
1378           val eqEqTempLocal = locals.makeLocal(ObjectReference, nme_EQEQ_LOCAL_VAR.mangledString, Object_Type, r.pos)
1379           val lNull    = new asm.Label
1380           val lNonNull = new asm.Label
1381 
1382           genLoad(l, ObjectReference)
1383           genLoad(r, ObjectReference)
1384           locals.store(eqEqTempLocal)
1385           bc dup ObjectReference
1386           genCZJUMP(lNull, lNonNull, Primitives.EQ, ObjectReference, targetIfNoJump = lNull)
1387 
1388           markProgramPoint(lNull)
1389           bc drop ObjectReference
1390           locals.load(eqEqTempLocal)
1391           genCZJUMP(success, failure, Primitives.EQ, ObjectReference, targetIfNoJump = lNonNull)
1392 
1393           markProgramPoint(lNonNull)
1394           locals.load(eqEqTempLocal)
1395           genCallMethod(Object_equals, InvokeStyle.Virtual)
1396           genCZJUMP(success, failure, Primitives.NE, BOOL, targetIfNoJump)
1397         }
1398       }
1399     }
1400

1403     def genLoadTry(tree: Try): BType

1405     def genInvokeDynamicLambda(ctor: Symbol, lambdaTarget: Symbol, environmentSize: Int, functionalInterface: Symbol): BType = {
1406       debuglog(s"Using invokedynamic rather than `new ${ctor.owner}`")
1407       val generatedType = classBTypeFromSymbol(functionalInterface)
1408       val isInterface = lambdaTarget.owner.isInterface
1409       val invokeStyle =
1410         if (lambdaTarget.isStaticMember) asm.Opcodes.H_INVOKESTATIC
1411         else if (lambdaTarget.isPrivate || lambdaTarget.isClassConstructor) asm.Opcodes.H_INVOKESPECIAL
1412         else if (isInterface) asm.Opcodes.H_INVOKEINTERFACE
1413         else asm.Opcodes.H_INVOKEVIRTUAL
1414 
1415       val targetHandle =
1416         new asm.Handle(invokeStyle,
1417           classBTypeFromSymbol(lambdaTarget.owner).internalName,
1418           lambdaTarget.name.mangledString,
1419           asmMethodType(lambdaTarget).descriptor,
1420           isInterface)
1421 
1422       val (a,b) = lambdaTarget.info.paramTypes.splitAt(environmentSize)
1423       var (capturedParamsTypes, lambdaParamTypes) = if(int.doLabmdasFollowJVMMetafactoryOrder) (a,b) else (b,a)
1424 
1425       if (invokeStyle != asm.Opcodes.H_INVOKESTATIC) capturedParamsTypes = lambdaTarget.owner.info :: capturedParamsTypes
1426 
1427       // Requires https://github.com/scala/scala-java8-compat on the runtime classpath
1428       val returnUnit = lambdaTarget.info.resultType.typeSymbol == UnitClass
1429       val functionalInterfaceDesc: String = generatedType.descriptor
1430       val desc = capturedParamsTypes.map(tpe => toTypeKind(tpe)).mkString(("("), "", ")") + functionalInterfaceDesc
1431       // TODO specialization
1432       val constrainedType = new MethodBType(lambdaParamTypes.map(p => toTypeKind(p)), toTypeKind(lambdaTarget.tpe.resultType)).toASMType
1433       val abstractMethod = functionalInterface.samMethod()
1434       val methodName = abstractMethod.name.mangledString
1435       val applyN = {
1436         val mt = asmMethodType(abstractMethod)
1437         mt.toASMType
1438       }
1439       bc.jmethod.visitInvokeDynamicInsn(methodName, desc, lambdaMetaFactoryBootstrapHandle,
1440         // boostrap args
1441         applyN, targetHandle, constrainedType
1442       )
1443 
1444       generatedType
1445     }
1446   }
1447   val lambdaMetaFactoryBootstrapHandle =
1448     new asm.Handle(asm.Opcodes.H_INVOKESTATIC,
1449       int.LambdaMetaFactory.javaBinaryName, int.MetafactoryName,
1450       "(Ljava/lang/invoke/MethodHandles$Lookup;Ljava/lang/String;Ljava/lang/invoke/MethodType;Ljava/lang/invoke/MethodType;Ljava/lang/invoke/MethodHandle;Ljava/lang/invoke/MethodType;)Ljava/lang/invoke/CallSite;",
1451       int.LambdaMetaFactory.isInterface)
1452 
1453 }
